\xe4\xbd\x86 Macro \xe4\xb8\x8e\xe5\x87\xbd\xe6\x95\xb0\xe6\x9c\x89\xe4\xbb\xa5\xe4\xb8\x8b\xe4\xb8\xa4\xe4\xb8\xaa\xe5\x8c\xba\xe5\x88\xab:\n\n1. \xe8\xaf\xa5\xe8\xa1\xa8\xe8\xbe\xbe\xe5\xbc\x8f\xe4\xbc\x9a\xe7\xab\x8b\xe5\x8d\xb3\xe8\xa2\xab\xe8\xa7\xa3\xe9\x87\x8a\xe5\x99\xa8\xe6\x89\xa7\xe8\xa1\x8c; \xe5\xb7\xa6\xe8\xbe\xb9\xe7\x9a\x84\xe9\x94\xae.\n\n\xe5\xbd\x93\xe5\x9c\xa8 Emacs \xe8\xbe\x93\xe5\x85\xa5 backquote \xe6\x97\xb6\xe4\xbc\x9a\xe6\x8f\x92\xe5\x85\xa5\xe4\xb8\xa4\xe4\xb8\xaa\xe5\x8f\x8d\xe5\xbc\x95\xe5\x8f\xb7, \xe5\x8f\xaf\xe4\xbb\xa5\xe4\xbd\xbf\xe7\x94\xa8\xe4\xbb\xa5\xe4\xb8\x8b\xe4\xbb\xa3\xe7\xa0\x81\xe5\x85\xb3\xe9\x97\xad\xe8\xbf\x99\xe4\xb8\xaa\xe5\x8a\x9f\xe8\x83\xbd:\n\n#+BEGIN_SRC emacs-lisp\n \xe7\x9a\x84\xe4\xbd\x9c\xe7\x94\xa8:\n\n#+BEGIN_SRC emacs-lisp\n  (defun my-print (number)\n    (message "This is a number: %d" number))\n\n  (my-print 2)               ; 1. output= This is a number: 2\n  (my-print (+ 2 3))         ; 2. output= This is a number: 5\n\n  (quote (+ 1 1))\n  ;; return a list= (+ 1 1)\n\n  (defmacro my-print-2 (number)\n    `(message "This is a number: %d" ,number))\n\n  (my-print-2 2)             ; 3. output= This is a number: 2\n  (my-print-2 (+ 2 3))       ; 4. output= This is a number: 5\n\n  (setq my-var 2)\n  (inc my-var)\n\n  (defmacro inc2 (var1 var2)\n    (list \'progn (list \'inc var1) (list \'inc var2)))\n\n  (macroexpand \'(inc2 my-var my-var))\n  (macroexpand-all \'(inc2 my-var my-var))\n#+END_SRC\n\nquote \xe4\xb8\x8d\xe5\xaf\xb9\xe8\xa1\xa8\xe8\xbe\xbe\xe5\xbc\x8f\xe8\xbf\x9b\xe8\xa1\x8c\xe6\xb1\x82\xe5\x80\xbc. \xe6\x89\x80\xe4\xbb\xa5\xe4\xbb\xa5\xe4\xb8\x8b\xe4\xbb\xa3\xe7\xa0\x81:\n\n#+BEGIN_SRC \xe8\xbf\x9b\xe8\xa1\x8c\xe6\xb1\x82\xe5\x80\xbc\xe8\xbf\x94\xe5\x9b\x9e 2, \xe8\x80\x8c\xe6\x98\xaf\xe8\xbf\x94\xe5\x9b\x9e\xe4\xb8\x80\xe4\xb8\xaa list.\n\nbackquote \xe5\x90\x8c\xe6\xa0\xb7\xe4\xb8\x8d\xe5\xaf\xb9\xe5\x90\x8e\xe9\x9d\xa2\xe7\x9a\x84\xe8\xa1\xa8\xe8\xbe\xbe\xe5\xbc\x8f\xe6\xb1\x82\xe5\x80\xbc, \xe4\xbd\x86\xe6\x98\xaf\xe5\xbd\x93 backquote \xe7\x94\xa8\xe9\x80\x97\xe5\x8f\xb7\xe4\xbf\xae\xe9\xa5\xb0\xe7\x9a\x84\xe5\x8f\x98\xe9\x87\x8f\xe5\xb0\x86\xe8\xbf\x9b\xe8\xa1\x8c\xe6\xb1\x82\xe5\x80\xbc.\n\n\xe4\xbe\x8b\xe5\xa6\x82\xe4\xbb\xa5\xe4\xb8\x8b\xe4\xbb\xa3\xe7\xa0\x81:\n\n#+BEGIN_SRC 3))\n#+END_SRC\n\n\xe5\xbd\x93\xe8\xbe\x93\xe5\x87\xba message \xe4\xb8\x94 number \xe4\xb8\x8d\xe5\xb8\xa6\xe9\x80\x97\xe5\x8f\xb7\xe6\x97\xb6, *my-print-2* \xe7\x9a\x84\xe6\x89\xa7\xe8\xa1\x8c\xe5\xb0\x86\xe6\x8f\x90\xe7\xa4\xba\xe9\x94\x99\xe8\xaf\xaf. \xe4\xb8\xba\xe4\xbb\x80\xe4\xb9\x88\xe4\xbd\xbf\xe7\x94\xa8\xe5\xae\x8f\n\n\xe4\xbd\xbf\xe7\x94\xa8\xe5\xae\x8f\xe5\x8f\xaf\xe4\xbb\xa5\xe5\x87\x8f\xe5\xb0\x91\xe9\x87\x8d\xe5\xa4\x8d\xe7\x9a\x84\xe4\xbb\xa3\xe7\xa0\x81, \xe4\xbb\xa5\xe4\xb8\x8b\xe6\x98\xaf\xe4\xb8\x80\xe4\xb8\xaa\xe4\xbd\xbf\xe7\x94\xa8\xe5\xae\x8f\xe6\x9d\xa5\xe5\xae\x9a\xe4\xb9\x89\xe5\x87\xbd\xe6\x95\xb0\xe7\x9a\x84\xe4\xbe\x8b\xe5\xad\x90:\n\n#+BEGIN_SRC emacs-lisp\n  (defun prelude-search (query-url prompt)\n    "Open the search url constructed with the QUERY-URL.\n  PROMPT sets the `read-string prompt."\n    (browse-url\n     (concat query-url\n             (url-hexify-string\n              (if mark-active\n                  (buffer-substring (region-beginning) (region-end))\n                (read-string prompt))))))\n\n  (defmacro prelude-install-search-engine (search-engine-name search-engine-url search-engine-prompt)                   ; #1\n    "Given some information regarding a search engine, install the interactive command to search through them"    \n    `(defun ,(intern (format "prelude-%s" search-engine-name)) ()                                                       ; #2\n         ,(format "Search %s with a query or region if any." search-engine-name)                                        ; #3\n         (interactive)\n         (prelude-search ,search-engine-url ,search-engine-prompt)))                                                    ; #4\n\n  (prelude-install-search-engine "google"     "http://www.google.com/search?q="              "Google: ")                ; #5\n  (prelude-install-search-engine "youtube"    "http://www.youtube.com/results?search_query=" "Search YouTube: ")\n  (prelude-install-search-engine "github"     "https://github.com/search?q="                 "Search GitHub: ")\n  (prelude-install-search-engine "duckduckgo" "https://duckduckgo.com/?t=lm&q="              "Search DuckDuckGo: ")\n#+END_SRC\n\n\xe4\xb8\x8b\xe9\x9d\xa2\xe5\xaf\xb9\xe4\xbb\xa5\xe4\xb8\x8a\xe4\xbb\xa3\xe7\xa0\x81\xe8\xbf\x9b\xe8\xa1\x8c\xe8\xae\xb2\xe8\xa7\xa3:\n\n\xe7\xac\xac#1 \xe8\xa1\x8c, \xe9\x80\x9a\xe8\xbf\x87 *prelude-install-search-engine* \xe5\xae\x9a\xe4\xb9\x89\xe4\xba\x86\xe4\xb8\x80\xe4\xb8\xaa\xe9\x9c\x80\xe8\xa6\x81 3 my-tags-updated-time (current-time))\n      (my-update-tags)\n      (message "updated tags after %d seconds." after-save-hook \xe4\xb8\xad, \xe6\x88\x96\xe8\x80\x85\xe7\xbb\x91\xe5\xae\x9a\xe5\x88\xb0\xe5\xbf\xab\xe6\x8d\xb7\xe9\x94\xae\xe4\xb8\x8a.\n\n***
